style=&quot;clear: both; text-align: center;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;separator&quot; style=&quot;clear: both; text-align: center;&quot;&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEjLCGYdIHSYPp0B6qIW9VwN-URfa73Wf2kKkpBANspBG-j_RryJDZcR8ud0YgtKoH_n450v_5Q_o8tX27XrZYmJ3bOTiWxUD4XjBdYcCMlDd_edn6ZnSFfxhx82zU_wtWgGDXB3H3awFvp6Dr0UayT_Hv7MV7-at2K1nY3N2L5nMc-MBSpOLL5e7VrIdw/s600/Most-Frequently-Asked-Questions-About-Email-Marketing-min.webp&quot; imageanchor=&quot;1&quot; style=&quot;margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;&quot;&gt;&lt;img alt=&quot;Most Frequently Asked Questions About Affiliate Marketing&quot; border=&quot;0&quot; data-original-height=&quot;338&quot; data-original-width=&quot;600&quot; height=&quot;360&quot; src=&quot;https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEjLCGYdIHSYPp0B6qIW9VwN-URfa73Wf2kKkpBANspBG-j_RryJDZcR8ud0YgtKoH_n450v_5Q_o8tX27XrZYmJ3bOTiWxUD4XjBdYcCMlDd_edn6ZnSFfxhx82zU_wtWgGDXB3H3awFvp6Dr0UayT_Hv7MV7-at2K1nY3N2L5nMc-MBSpOLL5e7VrIdw/w640-h360/Most-Frequently-Asked-Questions-About-Email-Marketing-min.webp&quot; title=&quot;Most Frequently Asked Questions About Affiliate Marketing&quot; width=&quot;640&quot; /&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;separator&quot; style=&quot;clear: both; text-align: center;&quot;&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;a name=&#39;more&#39;&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;There are lots of questions floating around about how affiliate marketing works, what to do and what not to do when it comes to setting up a business. With so much uncertainty surrounding both personal and business aspects of affiliate marketing. In this post, we will answer the most frequently asked question about affiliate marketing&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;h3 style=&quot;text-align: left;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;1. What is affiliate marketing?&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h3&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;&amp;nbsp;Affiliate marketing is a way to make money by promoting the products and services of other people and companies. You don&#39;t need to create your product or service, just promote existing ones. That&#39;s why it&#39;s so easy to get started with affiliate marketing. You can even get started with no budget at all!&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;h3 style=&quot;text-align: left;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;2. What is an affiliate program?&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h3&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;&amp;nbsp;An affiliate program is a package of information you create for your product, which is then made available to potential publishers. The program will typically include details about the product and its retail value, commission levels, and promotional materials. Many affiliate programs are managed via an affiliate network like ShareASale, which acts as a platform to connect publishers and advertisers, but it is also possible to offer your program directly.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;h4 style=&quot;text-align: left;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;3. What is an affiliate network and how do affiliate networks make money?&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;&amp;nbsp;Affiliate networks connect publishers to advertisers.&amp;nbsp; Affiliate networks make money by charging fees to the merchants who advertise with them; these merchants are known as advertisers. The percentage of each sale that the advertiser pays is negotiated between the merchant and the affiliate network.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;h4 style=&quot;text-align: left;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;4. What&#39;s the difference between affiliate marketing and dropshipping?&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;&amp;nbsp;Dropshipping is a method of selling that allows you to run an online store without having to stock products. You advertise the products as if you owned them, but when someone makes an order, you create a duplicate order with the distributor at a reduced price. The distributor takes care of the post and packaging on your behalf. As affiliate marketing is based on referrals and this type of drop shipping requires no investment in inventory when a customer buys through the affiliate link, no money exchanges hands.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;h4 style=&quot;text-align: left;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;&amp;nbsp;5. Can affiliate marketing and performance marketing be considered the same thing?&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;!--Ads Managed by AdSpyglass.com--&gt;
&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;&amp;nbsp;Performance marketing is a method of marketing that pays for performance, like when a sale is made or an ad is clicked This can include methods like PPC (pay-per-click) or display advertising. Affiliate marketing is one form of performance marketing where commissions are paid out to affiliates on a performance basis when they click on their affiliate link and make a purchase or action.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;h4 style=&quot;text-align: left;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;&amp;nbsp;6. Is it possible to promote affiliate offers on mobile devices?&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;&amp;nbsp;Smartphones are essentially miniature computers, so publishers can display the same websites and offers that are available on a PC. But mobiles also offer specific tools not available on computers, and these can be used to good effect for publishers. Publishers can optimize their ads for mobile users by making them easy to access by this audience. Publishers can also make good use of text and instant messaging to promote their offers. As the mobile market is predicted to make up 80% of traffic in the future, publishers who do not promote on mobile devices are missing out on a big opportunity.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;h4 style=&quot;text-align: left;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;7. Where do I find qualified publishers?&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;&amp;nbsp;The best way to find affiliate publishers is on reputable networks like ShareASale Cj(Commission Junction), Awin, and Impact radius. These networks have a strict application process and compliance checks, which means that all affiliates are trustworthy.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;h4 style=&quot;text-align: left;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;8. What is an affiliate disclosure statement?&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;&amp;nbsp;An affiliate disclosure statement discloses to the reader that there may be affiliate links on a website, for which a commission may be paid to the publisher if visitors follow these links and make purchases.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;h4 style=&quot;text-align: left;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;&amp;nbsp;9. Does social media activity play a significant role in affiliate marketing?&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;&amp;nbsp;Publishers promote their programs through a variety of means, including blogs, websites, email marketing, and pay-per-click ads. Social media has a huge interactive audience, making this platform a good source of potential traffic.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;h4 style=&quot;text-align: left;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;10. What is a super affiliate?&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;&amp;nbsp;A super affiliate is an affiliate partner who consistently drives a large majority of sales from any program they promote, compared to other affiliate partners involved in that program.&amp;nbsp; Affiliates make a lot of money from affiliate marketing Pat Flynn earned more than $50000 in 2013 from affiliate marketing.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;h4 style=&quot;text-align: left;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;11. How do we track publisher sales activity?&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;&amp;nbsp;Publishers can be identified by their publisher ID, which is used in tracking cookies to determine which publishers generate sales. The activity is then viewed within a network&#39;s dashboard.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;h4 style=&quot;text-align: left;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;&amp;nbsp;12. Could we set up an affiliate program in multiple countries?&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;&amp;nbsp;Because the Internet is so widespread, affiliate programs can be promoted in any country. Affiliate strategies that are set internationally need to be tailored to the language of the targeted country.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;h4 style=&quot;text-align: left;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;13. How can affiliate marketing help my business?&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;Affiliate marketing can help you grow your business in the following ways:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;ul style=&quot;text-align: left;&quot;&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;&amp;nbsp;It allows you to save time and money on marketing, which frees you up to focus on other aspects of your business.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;&amp;nbsp;You get access to friendly marketers who are eager to help you succeed.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;It also helps you to promote your products by sharing links and banners with a new audience.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;&amp;nbsp;It offers high ROI(Return on investment) and is cost-effective.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;h4 style=&quot;text-align: left;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;&amp;nbsp;14. How do I find quality publishers?&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;&amp;nbsp;One of the best ways to work with qualified affiliates is to hire an affiliate marketing agency that works with all the networks. Affiliates are carefully selected and go through a rigorous application process to be included in the network.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;h4 style=&quot;text-align: left;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;15. How Can we Promote Affiliate Links?&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;&amp;nbsp;Affiliate marketing is generally associated with websites, but there are other ways to promote your affiliate links, including:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;ul style=&quot;text-align: left;&quot;&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;A website or blog&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;Through email marketing and newsletter&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;Social media, like Facebook, Instagram, or Twitter.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;&amp;nbsp;Leave a comment on blogs or forums.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;Write an e-book or other digital product.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;Youtube&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;h4 style=&quot;text-align: left;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;&amp;nbsp;16. Do you have to pay to sign up for an affiliate program?&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;&amp;nbsp;To build your affiliate marketing business, you don&#39;t have to invest money in the beginning. You can sign up for free with any affiliate network and start promoting their brands right away.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;h4 style=&quot;text-align: left;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;17. What is a commission rate?&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;&amp;nbsp;Commission rates are typically based on a percentage of the total sale and in some cases can also be a flat fee for each transaction. The rates are set by the merchant.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;Who manages your affiliate program?&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;&amp;nbsp;Some merchants run their affiliate programs internally, while others choose to contract out management to a network or an external agency.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;h4 style=&quot;text-align: left;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;18. What is a cookie?&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;&amp;nbsp;Cookies are small pieces of data that work with web browsers to store information such as user preferences, login or registration data, and shopping cart contents. When someone clicks on your affiliate link, a cookie is placed on the user&#39;s computer or mobile device. That cookie is used to remember the link or ad that the visitor clicked on. Even if the user leaves your site and comes back a week later to make a purchase, you will still get credit for the sale and receive a commission it depends on the site cookies duration&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;h4 style=&quot;text-align: left;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;19. How long do cookies last?&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;&amp;nbsp;The merchant determines the duration of a cookie, also known as its “cookie life.” The most common length for an affiliate program is 30 days. If someone clicks on your affiliate link, you’ll be paid a commission if they purchase within 30 days of the click.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;h3 style=&quot;text-align: left;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;Final Saying&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h3&gt;&lt;div&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;Most new affiliates are eager to begin their affiliate marketing business. Unfortunately, there is a lot of bad information out there that can lead inexperienced affiliates astray. Hopefully, the answer to your question will provide clarity on how affiliate marketing works and the pitfalls you can avoid. Most importantly, keep in mind that success in affiliate marketing takes some time. Don&#39;t be discouraged if you&#39;re not immediately making sales or earning money. It takes most new affiliates months to make a full-time income.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</description><link>https://techncruncher.blogspot.com/2022/06/most-frequently-asked-questions-about.html</link><author>noreply@blogger.com (Unknown)</author><media:thumbnail xmlns:media="http://search.yahoo.com/mrss/" url="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEjLCGYdIHSYPp0B6qIW9VwN-URfa73Wf2kKkpBANspBG-j_RryJDZcR8ud0YgtKoH_n450v_5Q_o8tX27XrZYmJ3bOTiWxUD4XjBdYcCMlDd_edn6ZnSFfxhx82zU_wtWgGDXB3H3awFvp6Dr0UayT_Hv7MV7-at2K1nY3N2L5nMc-MBSpOLL5e7VrIdw/s72-w640-h360-c/Most-Frequently-Asked-Questions-About-Email-Marketing-min.webp" height="72" width="72"/><thr:total>2</thr:total></item><item><guid isPermaLink="false">tag:blogger.com,1999:blog-2525761963252134386.post-2614342552940509599</guid><pubDate>Mon, 18 Apr 2022 05:49:00 +0000</pubDate><atom:updated>2025-11-24T14:17:20.870+05:00</atom:updated><category domain="http://www.blogger.com/atom/ns#">Blockchain</category><title>What is Blockchain: Everything You Need to Know (2022)</title><description>&lt;table align=&quot;center&quot; style=&quot;clear: both; text-align: center;&quot;&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEhGSmMnm7rS8T3FdymStVEU4Vzq6neAfiH-HWZEh_NyxTReup8XF0S0N2hYBTI4xHAyV1-mWUv2CI-7PohYUMPpCIzoUm7GloDeFVR_-cquCFWMPp8vGgnG7TSsy6XPf9Gs-lG1lAWskhHGhc_2x7I5Y-psklBHqgNZQOPkcwqTNio0SXAUX5-hyRopZg/s1920/Most%20Frequently%20Asked%20Questions%20About%20Email%20Marketing.png&quot; style=&quot;margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;&lt;br /&gt;If you want to pay online, you need to register an account and provide credit card information. If you don&#39;t have a credit card, you can pay with bank transfer. With the rise of cryptocurrencies, these methods may become old.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;Imagine a world in which you can do transactions and many other things without having to give your personal information. A world in which you don’t need to rely on banks or governments anymore. Sounds amazing, right? That’s exactly what blockchain technology allows us to do.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;It’s like your computer’s hard drive. blockchain is a technology that lets you store data in digital blocks, which are connected together like links in a chain.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;Blockchain technology was originally invented in 1991 by two mathematicians, Stuart Haber and W. Scot Stornetta. They first proposed the system to ensure that timestamps could not be tampered with.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;A few years later, in 1998, software developer Nick Szabo proposed using a similar kind of technology to secure a digital payments system he called “Bit Gold.” However, this innovation was not adopted until Satoshi Nakamoto claimed to have invented the first Blockchain and Bitcoin.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;h3 style=&quot;text-align: left;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;So, What is Blockchain?&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h3&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;A blockchain is a distributed database shared between the nodes of a computer network. It saves information in digital format. Many people first heard of blockchain technology when they started to look up information about bitcoin.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;Blockchain is used in cryptocurrency systems to ensure secure, decentralized records of transactions.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;Blockchain allowed people to guarantee the fidelity and security of a record of data without the need for a third party to ensure accuracy.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;&lt;b&gt;To understand how a blockchain works, Consider these basic steps:&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;ul style=&quot;text-align: left;&quot;&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;Blockchain collects information in “blocks”.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;A block has a storage capacity, and once it&#39;s used up, it can be closed and linked to a previously served block.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;Blocks form chains, which are called “Blockchains.”&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;More information will be added to the block with the most content until its capacity is full. The process repeats itself.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;Each block in the chain has an exact timestamp and can&#39;t be changed.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;&lt;b&gt;Let’s get to know more about the blockchain.&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;h3 style=&quot;text-align: left;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;How does blockchain work?&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h3&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;Blockchain records digital information and distributes it across the network without changing it. The information is distributed among many users and stored in an immutable, permanent ledger that can&#39;t be changed or destroyed. That&#39;s why blockchain is also called &quot;Distributed Ledger Technology&quot; or DLT.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;Here’s how it works:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;ul style=&quot;text-align: left;&quot;&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;Someone or a computer will transacts&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;The transaction is transmitted throughout the network.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;A network of computers can confirm the transaction.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;When it is confirmed a transaction is added to a block&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;The blocks are linked together to create a history.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;script type=&quot;text/javascript&quot;&gt;

title=&quot;Grammarly vs prowritingaid&quot; width=&quot;640&quot; /&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/h2&gt;&lt;div style=&quot;text-align: left;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;&lt;b&gt;&lt;span&gt;&lt;a name=&#39;more&#39;&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/span&gt;ProWritingAid VS Grammarly:&lt;span style=&quot;color: #3c4043;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;background-color: white; font-size: 14px;&quot;&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;color: #3c4043; font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 14px;&quot;&gt;&amp;nbsp;When it comes to English grammar, there are two Big Players that everyone knows of: the Grammarly and ProWritingAid. but you are wondering which one to choose so here we write a detail article which will help you to choose the best one for you so Let&#39;s start&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;h2 style=&quot;text-align: left;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;What is Grammarly?&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h2&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;Grammarly is a tool that checks for grammatical errors, spelling, and punctuation.it gives you comprehensive feedback on your writing. You can use this tool to proofread and edit articles, blog posts, emails, etc.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;Grammarly also detects all types of mistakes, including sentence structure issues and misused words. It also gives you suggestions on style changes, punctuation, spelling, and grammar all are in real-time. The free version covers the basics like identifying grammar and spelling mistakes&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;whereas the Premium version offers a lot more functionality, it detects plagiarism in your content, suggests word choice, or adds fluency to it.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;h3 style=&quot;text-align: left;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;&lt;b&gt;Features of Grammarly&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h3&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;ul style=&quot;text-align: left;&quot;&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;&lt;b&gt;Spelling and Word Suggestion:&lt;/b&gt; Grammarly detects basic to advance grammatical errors and also help you why this is an error and suggest to you how you can improve it&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;&lt;b&gt;Create a Personal Dictionary:&lt;/b&gt; The Grammarly app allows you to add words to your personal dictionary so that the same mistake isn&#39;t highlighted every time you run Grammarly.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;&lt;b&gt;Different English Style&lt;/b&gt;: Check to spell for American, British, Canadian, and Australian English.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;&lt;b&gt;Plagiarism:&lt;/b&gt; This feature helps you detect if a text has been plagiarized by comparing it with over eight billion web pages.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;&lt;b&gt;Plugins:&lt;/b&gt; It offers Microsoft Word, Microsoft Outlook, and Google Chrome plugins.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;h2 style=&quot;text-align: left;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;What is ProWritingAid?&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h2&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;ProWritingAid is a style and grammar checker for content creators and writers. It helps to optimize word choice, punctuation errors, and common grammar mistakes, providing detailed reports to help you improve your writing.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;ProWritingAid can be used as an add-on to WordPress, Gmail, and Google Docs. The software also offers helpful articles, videos, quizzes, and explanations to help improve your writing.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;h3 style=&quot;text-align: left;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;Features of ProWriting Aid&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h3&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;Here are some key features of ProWriting Aid:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;ul style=&quot;text-align: left;&quot;&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;&lt;b&gt;Grammar checker and spell checker:&lt;/b&gt; This tool helps you to find all grammatical and spelling errors.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;&lt;b&gt;Find repeated words:&lt;/b&gt;&amp;nbsp; The tool also allows you to search for repeated words and phrases in your content.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;&lt;b&gt;Context-sensitive style suggestions:&lt;/b&gt;&amp;nbsp; You can find the exact style of writing you intend and suggest if it flows well in your writing.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;&lt;b&gt;Check the readability of your content:&lt;/b&gt; Pro Writing Aid helps you identify the strengths and weaknesses of your article by pointing out difficult sentences and paragraphs.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;&lt;b&gt;Sentence Length: &lt;/b&gt;It also indicates the length of your sentences.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;&lt;b&gt;Check Grammatical error:&lt;/b&gt; It also checks your work for any grammatical errors or typos, as well.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;&lt;b&gt;Overused words:&lt;/b&gt; As a writer, you might find yourself using the same word repeatedly. ProWritingAid&#39;s overused words checker helps you avoid this lazy writing mistake.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;&lt;b&gt;Consistency:&lt;/b&gt; Check your work for inconsistent usage of open and closed quotation marks.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;&lt;b&gt;Echoes:&lt;/b&gt; Check your writing for uniformly repetitive words and phrases.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;h3 style=&quot;text-align: left;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;Difference between Grammarly and Pro-Writing Aid&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h3&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;&lt;b&gt;Grammarly&lt;/b&gt; and &lt;b&gt;ProWritingAid&lt;/b&gt; are well-known grammar-checking software. However, if you&#39;re like most people who can&#39;t decide which to use, here are some different points that may be helpful in your decision.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;h3 style=&quot;text-align: left;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;Grammarly vs ProWritingAid&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h3&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;ul style=&quot;text-align: left;&quot;&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;&lt;b&gt;Grammarly &lt;/b&gt;is a writing enhancement tool that offers suggestions for grammar, vocabulary, and syntax whereas &lt;b&gt;ProWritingAid&lt;/b&gt; offers world-class grammar and style checking, as well as advanced reports to help you strengthen your writing.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;&lt;b&gt;Grammarly&lt;/b&gt; It can be quite useful for fiction writers.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;h2 style=&quot;text-align: left;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;ProWritingAid VS Grammarly: Pricing Difference&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h2&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;ul style=&quot;text-align: left;&quot;&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;ProWritingAid comes with three pricing structures. You also can opt for a monthly plan of $20.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;Grammarly offers a Premium subscription for $30/month for a monthly plan&amp;nbsp; $20/month for quarterly and $12/month for an annual subscription.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;The Business plan costs $12.50 Enterprise-level controls ensure that visual content remains on-brand, no matter how many people are working on it.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;h3 style=&quot;text-align: left;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;Audio&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h3&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;Create an animated image or video by adding audio to capture user’s attention in social news feeds.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;If you want to use audio from another stock site or your own audio tracks, you can upload them in the Uploads tab or from the more option.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;h3 style=&quot;text-align: left;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;Video&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h3&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;Want to create your own videos? And if you have a Canva Pro subscription, you can upload your brand’s custom colors and fonts to ensure designs stay on brand.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;h3 style=&quot;text-align: left;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;Logos&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h3&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;If you have a Canva Pro subscription, you’ll have a Logos tab. Here, you can upload variations of your brand logo to use throughout your designs.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;With Canva, you can also create your own logos. Note that you cannot trademark a logo with stock content in it.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;h3 style=&quot;text-align: left;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;Publishing with Canva&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h3&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;With Canva, free users can download and share designs to multiple platforms including Instagram, Facebook, Twitter, LinkedIn, Pinterest, Slack and Tumblr.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;Canva Pro subscribers can create multiple post formats from one design. For example, you can start by designing an Instagram post, and Canva&#39;s Magic Resizer can resize it for other networks, Stories, Reels, and other formats.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;Canva Pro subscribers can also use Canva’s Content Planner to post content on eight different accounts on Instagram, Facebook, Twitter, LinkedIn, Pinterest, Slack, and Tumblr.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;h3 style=&quot;text-align: left;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;Canva Team&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h3&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;Canva Pro allows you to work with your team on visual content. WordPress firewall and security scanner that keeps your site safe from malicious hackers, spam, and other online threats. This Plugin comes with a web application firewall (WAF) called tthread Defence&amp;nbsp; Feed&amp;nbsp; that helps to prevents brute force attacks by ensuring you set stronger passwords and limiting login attempts. It searches for malware and compares code, theme, and plugin files with the records in the WordPress.org repository to verify their integrity and reports changes to you.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;Wordfence security scanner provides you with actionable insights into your website&#39;s security status and will alert you to any potential threats, keeping it safe and secure. It also includes login security features that let you activate reCAPTCHA and two-factor authentication for your website.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;h3 style=&quot;text-align: left;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;Features in Bullets.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h3&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;ul style=&quot;text-align: left;&quot;&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;Scans your site for vulnerabilities.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;script type=&quot;text/javascript&quot;&gt;

Akismet&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h3&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;Akismet can help prevent spam from appearing on your site. Every day, it automatically checks every comment against a global database of spam to block malicious content. With Akismet, you also won’t have to worry about innocent comments being caught by the filter or false positives. You can simply tell Akismet about those and it will get better over time. It also checks your contact form submissions against its global spam database and weed out unnecessary fake information.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;h3 style=&quot;text-align: left;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;Features in Bullets:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h3&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;ul style=&quot;text-align: left;&quot;&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;The program automatically checks comments and filters out spam.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;Hidden or misleading links are often revealed in the comment body.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;Akismet tracks the status of each comment, allowing you to see which ones were caught by Akismet and which ones were cleared by a moderator.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;A spam-blocking feature that saves disk space and makes your site run faster.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;Moderators can view a list of comments approved by each user.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;h3 style=&quot;text-align: left;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;Pricing&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h3&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;ul style=&quot;text-align: left;&quot;&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;Free to use for personal blog&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;h3 style=&quot;text-align: left;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;5. Contact Form 7&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h3&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;Contact Form 7 is a plug-in that allows you to create contact forms that make it easy for your users to send messages to your site. The plug-in was developed by Takayuki Miyoshi and lets you create multiple contact forms on the same site; it also integrates Akismet spam filtering and lets you customize the styling and fields that you want to use in the form. The plug-in provides CAPTCHA and Ajax submitting.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;h3 style=&quot;text-align: left;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;Features in bullets:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h3&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;ul style=&quot;text-align: left;&quot;&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;Create and manage multiple contact forms&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;Easily customize form fields&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;Use simple markup to alter mail content&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;Add Lots of third-party extensions for additional functionality&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;Shortcode offers a way to insert content into pages or posts.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;Akismet spam filtering, Ajax-powered submitting, and CAPTCHA are all features of this plugin.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;h3 style=&quot;text-align: left;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;Pricing&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h3&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;ul style=&quot;text-align: left;&quot;&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;Free to use&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;h3 style=&quot;text-align: left;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;6. data-original-width=&quot;1920&quot; height=&quot;360&quot; src=&quot;https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/a/AVvXsEhQ__o2Bk7fjBlzcWaYTiBTTZ95DOPWpTIDWtMzAr9krA18i_9rwyAg6cHLKxIeFHR5Y194Rk7Xl8hXQYUME-yYDOGmLnm6LMvHEIRKdgBqcKD7348U3UE5l2a2T0s1xRm0id0LQOUoKvgeXl-QGtgUTwIyYeCR22MVLenD6zzunb9BG_Vhca6cJm3bAg=w640-h360&quot; title=&quot;NFTs&quot; width=&quot;640&quot; /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;Non-fungible tokens (NFTs) are the most popular digital assets today, capturing the attention of cryptocurrency investors, whales and people from around the world. People find it amazing that some users spend thousands or millions of dollars on a single NFT-based image of a monkey or other token, but you can simply take a screenshot for free. So here we share some freuently asked question about NFTs.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;h3 style=&quot;text-align: left;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;1) What is an NFT?&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h3&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;NFT stands for non-fungible&amp;nbsp; token, which is a cryptographic token on a blockchain with unique identification codes that distinguish it from other tokens. NFTs are unique and not interchangeable, which means no two NFTs are the same. NFTs can be a unique artwork, GIF, Images, videos, Audio album. in-game items, collectibles etc.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;h3 style=&quot;text-align: left;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;2) What is Blockchain?&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h3&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;A blockchain is a distributed digital ledger that allows for the secure storage of data. By recording any kind of information—such as bank account transactions, the ownership of Non-Fungible Tokens (NFTs), or Decentralized Finance (DeFi) smart contracts—in one place, and distributing it to many different computers, blockchains ensure that data can’t be manipulated without everyone in the system being aware.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;h3 style=&quot;text-align: left;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;3) What makes an NFT valuable?&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h3&gt;
&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;span&gt;&amp;nbsp;Non-fungible tokens have gained the hearts of people around the world, and they have given digital creators the recognition they deserve. One of the remarkable things about non-fungible tokens is that you can take a screenshot of one, but you don’t own it. This is because when a non-fungible token is created, then the transaction is stored on the blockchain, and the license or contract to hold such a token is awarded to the person owning the token in their digital wallet.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;You can sell your work and creations by attaching a license to it on the blockchain, where its ownership can be transferred. This lets you get exposure without losing full ownership of your work. Some of the most successful projects include Cryptopunks, Bored Ape Yatch Club NFTs, SandBox, World of Women and so on. These NFT projects have gained popularity globally and are owned by celebrities and other successful entrepreneurs. Owning one of these NFTs gives you an automatic ticket to exclusive business meetings and life-changing connections.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;h3 style=&quot;text-align: left;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;Final Saying&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h3&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;That’s a wrap. Hope you guys found this article enlightening. I just answer some question with my limited knowledge about NFTs. Click on (+From Store) to access chrome web store or simple search chrome web store and access it.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;separator&quot; style=&quot;clear: both; text-align: center;&quot;&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/a/AVvXsEgq7DjHt61IOEU5rrWvUcVSbatsb0GDTGri43l8qgHkbwoVPFYEAk7nWW9MpOm2Wr4AudzqPtQ9pOaGs9xyAR0-TR0HbsuJa8u_DOFYVIdowCsepPSGzoIvui2MArLLY10gnECpwodysbAMIL9LXXWPYguJLyEMCs9A6OegMeW4But4-AuOuMAN110plA=s1280&quot; style=&quot;margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;&lt;img border=&quot;0&quot; data-original-height=&quot;1280&quot; data-original-width=&quot;561&quot; height=&quot;289&quot; src=&quot;https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/a/AVvXsEgq7DjHt61IOEU5rrWvUcVSbatsb0GDTGri43l8qgHkbwoVPFYEAk7nWW9MpOm2Wr4AudzqPtQ9pOaGs9xyAR0-TR0HbsuJa8u_DOFYVIdowCsepPSGzoIvui2MArLLY10gnECpwodysbAMIL9LXXWPYguJLyEMCs9A6OegMeW4But4-AuOuMAN110plA=w140-h289&quot; width=&quot;140&quot; /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;4. Once you found an extension click on add to chrome a message will pop-up&amp;nbsp; asking if you wish to confirm your choice. Hit OK to install the extension in the Kiwi browser.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;separator&quot; style=&quot;clear: both; text-align: center;&quot;&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/a/AVvXsEjR1Au8lENnJDcBpf-vv28GffoBSEsK-i_LXN-CljyWPtSN01514RI_K3CqK0ClH3HC0kI86wi5AvQHgWt1Vis6t2gOsZtVtIFsB58ORG0HPsJo02U5K_Ae5M6LWqe6aZS7i8b-vWzyQKHra2yyk0Fg2zZ4OM-eAllebtKTTuWgivWlI1vNWYvu8rsEQQ=s854&quot; style=&quot;margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;&lt;img border=&quot;0&quot; data-original-height=&quot;854&quot; data-original-width=&quot;480&quot; height=&quot;296&quot; src=&quot;https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/a/AVvXsEjR1Au8lENnJDcBpf-vv28GffoBSEsK-i_LXN-CljyWPtSN01514RI_K3CqK0ClH3HC0kI86wi5AvQHgWt1Vis6t2gOsZtVtIFsB58ORG0HPsJo02U5K_Ae5M6LWqe6aZS7i8b-vWzyQKHra2yyk0Fg2zZ4OM-eAllebtKTTuWgivWlI1vNWYvu8rsEQQ=w180-h296&quot; width=&quot;180&quot; /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;5. height=&quot;360&quot; src=&quot;https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/a/AVvXsEgD5ya1-4Tnsum7tKBC7maSYhkX2x5tHg2-_ihpar1PmlsT7MKPH0419APpBlmOXCVkxaozFrSnC23BdOQy6AnChsLoBEDG2qt34GukCtnGjPXwGHpa9AicdbP0EjCMyxbTGYGUPz24NvoC6Ph3zCxOJ1ZhqxeAua4kx-SzwkbngPsWo9dciHSozTstJA=w640-h360&quot; width=&quot;640&quot; /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;div&gt;&lt;h3 style=&quot;text-align: left;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;&lt;span&gt;&lt;a name=&#39;more&#39;&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/span&gt;1. Why is email marketing important?&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h3&gt;&lt;div&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;Email is the marketing tool that helps you&amp;nbsp; create a seamless, connected, frictionless buyer journey. More importantly, email marketing allows you to build relationships with prospects, customers, and past customers. It&#39;s your chance to speak&amp;nbsp; to them right in their inbox, at a time that suits them. Along with the right message, email can become one of your most powerful marketing channels.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;h3 style=&quot;text-align: left;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;2. What is benefits of email marketing?&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h3&gt;&lt;div&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;Email marketing is best way for creating long term relationship with your clients, and increasing sales in our company.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;Benefits of email marketing for bussiness:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div&gt;&lt;ul style=&quot;text-align: left;&quot;&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;Better brand recognition&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;Statistics of what works best&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;More sales&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;Targeted audience&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;More traffic to your products/services/newsletter&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;Build credibility&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;Most&amp;nbsp; bussinesses are using email marketing and making tons of money with email marketing.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;h3 style=&quot;text-align: left;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;3. What is the simplest day and time to send my marketing emails?&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h3&gt;&lt;div&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;Again, the answer to this question varies from company to company. And again, testing is the way to find out what works best. Typically, weekends and mornings seem to be&amp;nbsp; times when multiple emails are opened, but since your audience may have different habits, it&#39;s best to experiment and then use your&amp;nbsp; data to decide.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;h3 style=&quot;text-align: left;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;&amp;nbsp;4. Which metrics should I be looking at?&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h3&gt;&lt;div&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;The two most important metrics for email marketing are&amp;nbsp; open rate and click-through rate. If your emails aren&#39;t opened, subscribers will never see your full marketing message, and if they open them but don&#39;t click through to your site, your emails won&#39;t convert.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;h3 style=&quot;text-align: left;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;5. How do I write a decent subject line?&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h3&gt;&lt;div&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;The best subject lines are short and to the point, accurately describing&amp;nbsp; the content of the email, but also catchy and intriguing, so the reader wants to know more. Once Again, this is the perfect place for&amp;nbsp; A/B testing, to see what types of subject lines work best with your audience. Your call to action should be clear and&amp;nbsp; simple. It should be somewhere at the top of your email for those who haven&#39;t finished reading the entire email,&amp;nbsp; then repeated&amp;nbsp; at the end for those reading all the way through. It should state exactly what you want subscribers to do, for example &quot;Click here to download the premium theme for free.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;h3 style=&quot;text-align: left;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
  &lt;div id=&quot;atContainer-05a47ba863f62ec113e14b51b976d14a&quot;&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;h3 style=&quot;text-align: left;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;8. How do I prevent audience from unsubscribing?&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h3&gt;&lt;div&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;If the&amp;nbsp; subject line of the email is irrelevant to&amp;nbsp; customers, they will ignore it multiple times. But, if it keeps repeating, they are intercepted and unsubscribed from your emails. So, send relevant emails for the benefit of the customer. Don&#39;t send emails that often only focus&amp;nbsp; on sales, offers and discounts.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;Submit information about your business and offers so you can connect with customers. You can also update them on recent trends in your industry. The basic role of an email is first and foremost to&amp;nbsp; connect with customers, get the most out of this tool.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;h3 style=&quot;text-align: left;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;9. What is the difference between a cold email and a spam email?&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h3&gt;&lt;div&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;Cold emails are mostly sales emails that are sent with content align to the needs of the recipient. It is usually personalized and includes a business perspective. However, it is still an unsolicited email. And all unsolicited emails are marked as SPAM.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;Regularly receiving this type of unsolicited email in your users&#39; inboxes, chances are&amp;nbsp; your emails will soon be diverted to&amp;nbsp; spam or junk folders. The most important thing to prevent this from happening is to respect your recipients&#39; choice to opt-out of receiving emails from you. You can add the links to easily unsubscribe. You must be familiar with the CAN-SPAM Act and its regulations.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;h3 style=&quot;text-align: left;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;10. Where can I find email template?&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h3&gt;&lt;div&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;Almost all email campaign tools provide you with ready-made templates. Whether you use MailChimp or Pardot, you&#39;ll get several email templates ready to use.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;&amp;nbsp;However, if you want to create a template from scratch, you can do so.Most of email campaign tools have option to paste the HTML code of your own design.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;h3 style=&quot;text-align: left;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;&lt;br /&gt;11. What email marketing trend will help marketers succeed in 2022?&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h3&gt;&lt;div&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;Is it a trend to listen to&amp;nbsp; and get to know your customers? I think people realize how bad it feels for a brand or a company to obsess over themselves without knowing their customers personal needs. People who listen empathetically and then provide value based on what they learn will win.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;h3 style=&quot;text-align: left;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;&lt;span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span&gt;Final Saying&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h3&gt;&lt;div&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: Comfortaa;&quot;&gt;&amp;nbsp;You can approach email marketing in different ways.
